wxl 2316$61 – 2023 ckjdß ui 27 jeks isl=rdod – 2023'01'27
No. 2316/61 – FRIDAY, JANUARY  27, 2023
SRI  LANKA  INSTITUTE  OF  ARCHITECTS
NEW Registration and Renewal of Registration of “Chartered Arch itects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” 
for the year 2023/2024 under the Architects Registration Board,  established as per the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects 
(Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996.
   Reference is made to the notes appearing on pages 1A, 2A, 3A , 4A and 5A of the Gazette (Extraordinary) No. 1015/19 
of Friday, the 20th February, 1998 of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka with regard to the Registration of 
persons who are eligible to practice Architecture in Sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and 
“Architectural Licentiates”. The interpretations of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects (Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996 in 
the above Gazette Notiﬁ cation will apply in all respects to the list published below.
   The Architects Registration Board of the Sri Lanka Institute  of Architects as per the functions and powers vested upon 
it by the said Act. of Parliament, has now prepared the list of  the “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural 
Licentiates” who are eligible to be Gazetted for the Year 2023/2024 (01st February 2023 to 31st January 2024).
   The Architects Registration Board directed me to publish the  Names, Addresses and Registration Numbers of the 
“Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” who have been registered as given below. This registration 
expires on 31st January 2024.
 N. W. W. Wංඃൾ඄ඈඈඇ,
 Registrar.
Architects Registration Board
Sri Lanka Institute of Architects,
No. 120/7, Vidya Mawatha,
Colombo 07,
27th January 2023.
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
1A – PG6193 – 1506 (01/2023)
